                        }, {

                        }, {

                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-22",
                            "value": 1731.91
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-23",

                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-24",

                            "time": "2026-06-25",
                            "value": 1736.31
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-26",
                            "value": 1737.65
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-29",
                            "value": 1739.12
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-06-30",
                            "value": 1740.48
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-07-01",
                            "value": 1741.84
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-07-02",
                            "value": 1743.15
                        }, {
                            "time": "2026-07-03",
                            "value": 1744.59
                        }],
                        "fetched_at": "2026-07-06T03:38:56+00:00"
                    };
                    const tradeLevels = {
                        "entry": 1904.8,
                        "stop": 1852.42,
                        "target": 2080.8
                    };
                    const el = document.getElementById('swg-chart');
                    let chart = null;
                    let candleSeries = null;
                    const maSeries = {};
                    let priceLines = [];

                    function clearPriceLines() {
                        if (!candleSeries)
                            return;
                        priceLines.forEach(line => {
                            try {
                                candleSeries.removePriceLine(line);
                            } catch (e) {}
                        }
                        );
                        priceLines = [];
                    }

                    function addPriceLine(price, color, title) {
                        if (!candleSeries || price === null || price === undefined || !Number.isFinite(Number(price)))
                            return;
                        const line = candleSeries.createPriceLine({
                            price: Number(price),
                            color,
                            lineWidth: 1,
                            lineStyle: 2,
                            axisLabelVisible: true,
                            title,
                        });
                        priceLines.push(line);
                    }

                    function applyTradeLevels() {
                        clearPriceLines();
                        if (!tradeLevels)
                            return;
                        addPriceLine(tradeLevels.stop, '#ef4444', 'Stop');
                        addPriceLine(tradeLevels.target, '#22c55e', 'Target');
                        if (tradeLevels.entry > 0) {
                            addPriceLine(tradeLevels.entry, '#93c5fd', 'Entry');
                        }
                        const stopLeg = document.getElementById('swg-leg-stop');
                        const tgtLeg = document.getElementById('swg-leg-target');
                        if (stopLeg)
                            stopLeg.hidden = tradeLevels.stop === null;
                        if (tgtLeg)
                            tgtLeg.hidden = tradeLevels.target === null;
                    }

                    function ensureChart() {
                        if (chart || !el || typeof LightweightCharts === 'undefined') {
                            if (el && typeof LightweightCharts === 'undefined') {
                                el.innerHTML = '<p style="padding:1rem;color:#fca5a5;font-size:0.82rem">Chart library failed to load.</p>';
                            }
                            return;
                        }
                        chart = LightweightCharts.createChart(el, {
                            width: el.clientWidth,
                            height: 400,
                            layout: {
                                background: {
                                    type: 'solid',
                                    color: '#1e2838'
                                },
                                textColor: '#8fa3bc'
                            },
                            grid: {
                                vertLines: {
                                    color: 'rgba(46,61,84,0.55)'
                                },
                                horzLines: {
                                    color: 'rgba(46,61,84,0.55)'
                                }
                            },
                            rightPriceScale: {
                                borderColor: '#2e3d54'
                            },
                            timeScale: {
                                borderColor: '#2e3d54',
                                timeVisible: true,
                                secondsVisible: false
                            },
                            crosshair: {
                                mode: LightweightCharts.CrosshairMode.Normal
                            },
                            localization: {
                                timeFormatter: (t) => {
                                    const d = new Date(t * 1000);
                                    const opts = {
                                        timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata',
                                        month: 'short',
                                        day: '2-digit'
                                    };
                                    if (activeTf === '1h') {
                                        opts.hour = '2-digit';
                                        opts.minute = '2-digit';
                                    }
                                    return d.toLocaleString('en-IN', opts);
                                }
                                ,
                            },
                        });
                        candleSeries = chart.addCandlestickSeries({
                            upColor: '#22c55e',
                            downColor: '#ef4444',
                            borderUpColor: '#22c55e',
                            borderDownColor: '#ef4444',
                            wickUpColor: '#22c55e',
                            wickDownColor: '#ef4444',
                        });
                        const defs = {
                            sma9: {
                                color: '#ef4444',
                                title: 'SMA-9'
                            },
                            sma20: {
                                color: '#3b82f6',
                                title: 'SMA-20'
                            },
                            sma50: {
                                color: '#f59e0b',
                                title: 'SMA-50'
                            },
                            sma200: {
                                color: '#22c55e',
                                title: 'SMA-200'
                            },
                            ema21: {
                                color: '#a78bfa',
                                title: 'EMA-21'
                            },
                        };
                        Object.entries(defs).forEach( ([key,cfg]) => {
                            maSeries[key] = chart.addLineSeries({
                                color: cfg.color,
                                lineWidth: 2,
                                title: cfg.title,
                                priceLineVisible: false,
                                lastValueVisible: false,
                            });
                        }
                        );
                        new ResizeObserver( () => chart && chart.applyOptions({
                            width: el.clientWidth
                        })).observe(el);
                    }

                    function updateLegend(payload) {
                        const hourly = payload.intraday === true || payload.interval === '1h';
                        document.querySelectorAll('#swg-chart-legend [data-series]').forEach(node => {
                            const key = node.getAttribute('data-series');
                            const hasData = Array.isArray(payload[key]) && payload[key].length > 0;
                            if (key === 'sma200') {
                                node.hidden = hourly || !hasData;
                            } else if (key === 'ema21') {
                                node.hidden = !hourly || !hasData;
                            } else if (key === 'sma9' || key === 'sma20' || key === 'sma50') {
                                node.hidden = !hasData;
                            }
                        }
                        );
                        const intervalEl = document.getElementById('swg-chart-interval');
                        const rangeEl = document.getElementById('swg-chart-range');
                        const barsEl = document.getElementById('swg-chart-bars');
                        if (intervalEl)
                            intervalEl.textContent = payload.interval || (hourly ? '1h' : '1d');
                        if (rangeEl)
                            rangeEl.textContent = payload.range || activeTf;
                        if (barsEl)
                            barsEl.textContent = String((payload.bars || []).length);
                    }

                    function setChartData(payload) {
                        if (!payload || !payload.bars || !payload.bars.length)
                            return;
                        ensureChart();
                        if (!candleSeries)
                            return;
                        candleSeries.setData(payload.bars);
                        const hourly = payload.intraday === true || payload.interval === '1h';
                        const keys = hourly ? ['sma9', 'sma20', 'sma50', 'ema21'] : ['sma9', 'sma20', 'sma50', 'sma200'];
                        keys.forEach(key => {
                            if (maSeries[key]) {
                                maSeries[key].setData(payload[key] || []);
                            }
                        }
                        );
                        if (!hourly && maSeries.ema21)
                            maSeries.ema21.setData([]);
                        if (hourly && maSeries.sma200)
                            maSeries.sma200.setData([]);
                        chart.timeScale().fitContent();
                        updateLegend(payload);
                        applyTradeLevels();
                    }

                    async function loadTimeframe(tf) {
                        activeTf = tf;
                        document.querySelectorAll('#swg-tf-tabs button').forEach(btn => {
                            const on = btn.getAttribute('data-tf') === tf;
                            btn.classList.toggle('active', on);
                            btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', on ? 'true' : 'false');
                            btn.disabled = on;
                        }
                        );
                        try {
                            const r = await fetch('swing-chart-api.php?symbol=' + encodeURIComponent(SYMBOL) + '&tf=' + encodeURIComponent(tf), {
                                credentials: 'same-origin',
                            });
                            const data = await r.json();
                            if (!data.ok || !data.chart) {
                                throw new Error(data.error || 'Chart load failed');
                            }
                            setChartData(data.chart);
                        } catch (e) {
                            const meta = document.getElementById('swg-chart-meta');
                            if (meta)
                                meta.textContent = 'Chart error: ' + (e.message || 'unknown');
                        } finally {
                            document.querySelectorAll('#swg-tf-tabs button').forEach(btn => {
                                btn.disabled = false;
                            }
                            );
                            document.querySelectorAll('#swg-tf-tabs button[data-tf="' + tf + '"]').forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.add('active');
                            }
                            );
                        }
                    }

                    document.querySelectorAll('#swg-tf-tabs button').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                            const tf = btn.getAttribute('data-tf');
                            if (!tf || tf === activeTf)
                                return;
                            loadTimeframe(tf);
                        }
                        );
                    }
                    );

                    setChartData(initialChart);
                }
                )();
            </script>

            <script>
                function swgSyncModeFields() {
                    const mode = document.querySelector('input[name="mode"]:checked')?.value || 'symbol';
                    const uni = mode === 'universe';
                    const etf = mode === 'etf';
                    const scanMode = uni || etf;
                    const bt = mode === 'backtest';
                    const sym = mode === 'symbol';
                    const symInput = document.querySelector('input[name="symbol"]');
                    const show = (id, on) => {
                        const el = document.getElementById(id);
                        if (el)
                            el.style.display = on ? '' : 'none';
                    }
                    ;
                    show('symbol-field', sym);
                    show('universe-field', uni);
                    show('etf-category-field', etf);
                    show('max-scan-field', uni);
                    show('min-verdict-field', scanMode);
                    show('sort-field', scanMode);
                    show('zone-52w-field', uni);
                    show('breakout-volume-field', uni);
                    show('gc9-only-field', scanMode);
                    show('async-scan-field', uni);
                    show('entry-price-field', sym);
                    show('entry-date-field', sym);
                    show('backtest-symbols-field', bt);
                    show('backtest-max-field', bt);
                    show('backtest-fund-field', bt);
                    show('backtest-demo-field', bt);
                    const etfRef = document.getElementById('swg-etf-reference');
                    if (etfRef)
                        etfRef.style.display = etf ? '' : 'none';
                    if (symInput) {
                        if (sym) {
                            symInput.setAttribute('required', 'required');
                        } else {
                            symInput.removeAttribute('required');
                        }
                    }
                }
                document.querySelectorAll('input[name="mode"]').forEach(el => {
                    el.addEventListener('change', swgSyncModeFields);
                }
                );
                swgSyncModeFields();
                (function() {
                    const tabs = document.getElementById('swg-etf-cat-tabs');
                    const table = document.getElementById('swg-etf-hits-table');
                    if (!tabs || !table)
                        return;
                    tabs.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                            const cat = btn.getAttribute('data-cat') || 'all';
                            tabs.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('active', b === btn));
                            table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr').forEach(tr => {
                                const rowCat = tr.getAttribute('data-cat') || '';
                                tr.hidden = cat !== 'all' && rowCat !== cat;
                            }
                            );
                        }
                        );
                    }
                    );
                }
                )();
            </script>
